       <div id="cp-main">
        <h3 id="cp-lede">
         Red Carpet Watch
        </h3>
        <div class="cp-story-header oscars-2015">
         <h1 id="cp-title">
          Oscars 2015
         </h1>
        </div>
        <h3 class="interstitial ">
         Noteworthy Looks
        </h3>
        <article class="cp-block clear odd" data-idx="1" data-short-url="" itemid="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/julianne-moore" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/NewsArticle">
         <div class="cp-image photo ">
          <figure aria-label="media" class="photo media media-100000003529140 layout-large-horizontal ratio-tall" data-media-action="modal" id="media-100000003529140" itemid="http://i1.nyt.com/images/2015/02/22/fashion/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-ZLB7/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-ZLB7-jumbo.jpg" itemprop="associatedMedia image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" role="group">
           <span class="visually-hidden">
            Photo
           </span>
           <div class="image">
            <img alt="" class="media-viewer-candidate" data-mediaviewer-caption="" data-mediaviewer-credit="Photographs by Noel West for The New York Times" data-mediaviewer-src="http://i1.nyt.com/images/2015/02/22/fashion/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-ZLB7/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-ZLB7-jumbo.jpg" itemprop="url" src="http://i1.nyt.com/images/2015/02/22/fashion/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-ZLB7/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-ZLB7-jumbo.jpg"/>
            <meta content="422" itemprop="height"/>
            <meta content="495" itemprop="width"/>
           </div>
           <figcaption class="caption" itemprop="caption description">
            <span class="credit" itemprop="copyrightHolder">
             <span class="visually-hidden">
              Credit
             </span>
             Photographs by Noel West for The New York Times
            </span>
           </figcaption>
          </figure>
         </div>
         <div class="cp-text photo " id="cp-block-54ea70ad61646d76d70e0000">
          <h6 class="cp-date">
           <a class="cp-date-a" datetime="2015-03-19T11:16:06+00:00" href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/julianne-moore">
            June 17, 2015
           </a>
          </h6>
          <h2 class="cp-celeb" itemprop="headline name">
           <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/julianne-moore" itemprop="url">
            Julianne Moore
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="cp-desc" itemprop="articleBody description text">
           <p>
            Ms. Moore did edgy  on Saturday. At the Independent Spirit Awards, she wore a Dior Haute Couture minidress that appeared to be constructed out of shiny candy wrappers. She has a very open mind, and she loves to take risks, her stylist, Leslie Fremar, told
            <a href="http://nyti.ms/19MRVbg">
             The Times's Alexandra Jacobs
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            On Sunday night, which was Ms. Moore's turn to take the trophy after five nominations, she set risk aside. Her floral embroidered Chanel Haute Couture gown was the picture of uncontroversial awards-season elegance. "Karl Lagerfeld made this for me," she said on the red carpet. An offer like that is hard to refuse.
           </p>
           <p>
            <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/julianne-moore">
             See more of her looks.
            </a>
           </p>
          </div>
          <ul class="cp-related">
          </ul>
          <div aria-label="tools" class="tone-standard sharetools theme-classic sharetools-story-meta layout-horizontal" data-description="Ms. Moore did edgy  on Saturday. At the Independent Spirit Awards, she wore a Dior Haute Couture minidress that appeared to be constructed out of shiny candy wrappers. She has a very open mind, and s..." data-media="http://i1.nyt.com/images/2015/02/22/fashion/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-ZLB7/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-ZLB7-facebookJumbo.jpg" data-shares="facebook|,twitter|,pinterest|,show-all|more" data-slug="julianne-moore" data-title="Red Carpet Watch | Oscars 2015 | Julianne Moore | NYTimes.com" data-url="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/julianne-moore" role="group">
           <span class="sharetools-label visually-hidden">
            Share This Page
           </span>
          </div>
          <!-- close shareTools -->
         </div>
        </article>
        <article class="cp-block clear" data-idx="2" data-short-url="" itemid="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/emma-stone" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/NewsArticle">
         <div class="cp-image photo ">
          <figure aria-label="media" class="photo media media-100000003529179 layout-large-horizontal ratio-tall" data-media-action="modal" id="media-100000003529179" itemid="http://i2.nyt.com/images/2015/02/22/fashion/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-EZJ9/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-EZJ9-jumbo.jpg" itemprop="associatedMedia image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" role="group">
           <span class="visually-hidden">
            Photo
           </span>
           <div class="image">
            <img alt="" class="media-viewer-candidate" data-mediaviewer-caption="" data-mediaviewer-credit="Photographs by Noel West for The New York Times" data-mediaviewer-src="http://i2.nyt.com/images/2015/02/22/fashion/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-EZJ9/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-EZJ9-jumbo.jpg" itemprop="url" src="http://i2.nyt.com/images/2015/02/22/fashion/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-EZJ9/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-EZJ9-jumbo.jpg"/>
            <meta content="422" itemprop="height"/>
            <meta content="495" itemprop="width"/>
           </div>
           <figcaption class="caption" itemprop="caption description">
            <span class="credit" itemprop="copyrightHolder">
             <span class="visually-hidden">
              Credit
             </span>
             Photographs by Noel West for The New York Times
            </span>
           </figcaption>
          </figure>
         </div>
         <div class="cp-text photo " id="cp-block-54ea7b7a61646d672e0a0000">
          <h6 class="cp-date">
           <a class="cp-date-a" datetime="2015-03-19T11:16:06+00:00" href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/emma-stone">
            June 17, 2015
           </a>
          </h6>
          <h2 class="cp-celeb" itemprop="headline name">
           <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/emma-stone" itemprop="url">
            Emma Stone
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="cp-desc" itemprop="articleBody description text">
           <p>
            Ms. Stone shot to the top of best-dressed lists after the Golden Globe awards, when she did the unthinkable: she wore pants. She took the more traditional route for Oscar night  a floor-length gown, properly glittery  but it isn't every young actress who could carry off acid green.
           </p>
           <p>
            Elie Saab, the Lebanese couturier who is a red-carpet mainstay (Halle Berry accepted her Best Actress Oscar wearing a Saab gown), designed the dress. But equal credit has to go to Ms. Stone, who pulled it off with aplomb.
           </p>
           <p>
            <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/emma-stone">
             See more of her looks.
            </a>
           </p>
          </div>
          <ul class="cp-related">
          </ul>
          <div aria-label="tools" class="tone-standard sharetools theme-classic sharetools-story-meta layout-horizontal" data-description="Ms. Stone shot to the top of best-dressed lists after the Golden Globe awards, when she did the unthinkable: she wore pants. She took the more traditional route for Oscar night  a floor-length gown, p..." data-media="http://i2.nyt.com/images/2015/02/22/fashion/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-EZJ9/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-EZJ9-facebookJumbo.jpg" data-shares="facebook|,twitter|,pinterest|,show-all|more" data-slug="emma-stone" data-title="Red Carpet Watch | Oscars 2015 | Emma Stone | NYTimes.com" data-url="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/emma-stone" role="group">

           </span>

        <article class="cp-block clear odd ad-photo" data-idx="3" data-short-url="" itemid="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/reese-witherspoon" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/NewsArticle">
         <div class="clear cp-image photo ">

          <div class="cp-text photo " id="cp-block-54ea77ca61646d6732020000">
           <h6 class="cp-date">
            <a class="cp-date-a" href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/reese-witherspoon">
             June 17, 2015
            </a>
           </h6>
           <h2 class="cp-celeb" itemprop="headline name">
            <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/reese-witherspoon" itemprop="url">
             Reese Witherspoon
            </a>
           </h2>
           <div class="cp-desc" itemprop="articleBody description text">
            <p>
             Tom Ford's name has been in the air this Oscar season. In a move that seemed to acknowledge a truth not universally acknowledged  that star power, as much as industry validation, drives fashion sales  Mr. Ford moved his women's wear show from London Fashion Week, currently underway in Britain, to Los Angeles, where it was held last night to a crowd thick with celebrity fans.
            </p>
            <p>
             Mr. Ford didn't sweep the Oscars red carpet this evening, but the look he got was worth a passel of also-rans. Reese Witherspoon, a nominee for her role in "Wild," wore a simple white dress with black accent details by Mr. Ford. It was one of the evening's big winners, even if she didn't get the Oscar.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/reese-witherspoon">
              See more of her looks.
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

         <div class="cp-text photo " id="cp-block-54ea67bb61646d6393060000">
          <h6 class="cp-date">
           <a class="cp-date-a" datetime="2015-03-19T11:16:06+00:00" href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/melanie-griffith-and-dakota-johnson">
            June 17, 2015
           </a>
          </h6>
          <h2 class="cp-celeb" itemprop="headline name">
           <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/melanie-griffith-and-dakota-johnson" itemprop="url">
            Dakota Johnson
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="cp-desc" itemprop="articleBody description text">
           <p>
            The Oscars novice of the year is not a nominee  not yet. But Ms. Johnson, currently riding a wave of notoriety from "Fifty Shades of Grey," emerged from the awards as a style star in the making. She wasn't the only actress to wear Saint Laurent; Margot Robbie, the Australian up-and-comer from last year's "Wolf of Wall Street," did, too. But Ms. Johnson made the grunge-leaning Saint Laurent look both fresh and classy on the red carpet, making a complicated one-shouldered silhouette and a hard color look (dumb fashion word coming, sorry) effortless.
           </p>
           <p>
            She's still getting her sea legs on the carpet, to judge from the awkward interviews she gave to the Seacrest posse. But she's got style, at least, to run circles around many actors and actresses with years more experience.
           </p>
          </div>
          <ul class="cp-related">
          </ul>
          <div aria-label="tools" class="tone-standard sharetools theme-classic sharetools-story-meta layout-horizontal" data-description="The Oscars novice of the year is not a nominee  not yet.          <div class="cp-text photo " id="cp-block-54ea6ebb61646d63970c0000">
          <h6 class="cp-date">
           <a class="cp-date-a" datetime="2015-03-19T11:16:06+00:00" href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/lupita-nyong-o">
            June 17, 2015
           </a>
          </h6>
          <h2 class="cp-celeb" itemprop="headline name">
           <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/lupita-nyong-o" itemprop="url">
            Lupita Nyong'o
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="cp-desc" itemprop="articleBody description text">
           <p>
            When she was nominated for an Academy Award last year, Ms. Nyong'o approached the red-carpet circuit leading up to the big event with what my colleague Guy Trebay called
            <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/2014/04/13/fashion/lupita-nyongo-beauty-lancome.html.">
             "military precision"
            </a>
            (The campaign was successful, netting both an Oscar and a lucrative Lancme contract for the star.)
           </p>
           <p>
            This year, Ms. Nyong'o didn't have the pressure of a nomination, but she didn't slack in the dress department. Her gown, a custom design by Francisco Costa of Calvin Klein Collection, was liberally studded with natural pearls, some 6,000 according to published reports. It must have weighed a ton. But Ms. Nyong'o, by now a veteran warrior of the red-carpet wars, proved that she's no slouch.
           </p>
          </div>
          <ul class="cp-related">
          </ul>
          <div aria-label="tools" class="tone-standard sharetools theme-classic sharetools-story-meta layout-horizontal" data-description="When she was nominated for an Academy Award last year, Ms. Nyong'o approached the red-carpet circuit leading up to the big event with what my colleague Guy Trebay called &quot;military precision&quot; ..." data-media="http://i1.nyt.com/images/2015/02/22/fashion/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-0ALQ/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-0ALQ-facebookJumbo.jpg" data-shares="facebook|,twitter|,pinterest|,show-all|more" data-slug="lupita-nyong-o" data-title="Red Carpet Watch | Oscars 2015 | Lupita Nyong'o | NYTimes.com" data-url="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/lupita-nyong-o" role="group">

         <div class="cp-text photo " id="cp-block-54ea69bf61646d6397090000">
          <h6 class="cp-date">
           <a class="cp-date-a" datetime="2015-03-19T11:16:06+00:00" href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/marion-cotillard">
            June 17, 2015
           </a>
          </h6>
          <h2 class="cp-celeb" itemprop="headline name">
           <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/marion-cotillard" itemprop="url">
            Marion Cotillard
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="cp-desc" itemprop="articleBody description text">
           <p>
            You can set your watch by Ms. Cotillard's red-carpet choices  provided that it's a Dior watch. Ms. Cotillard, a longtime ambassador for the label, is, with few exceptions, brand faithful. But the Dior designer Raf Simons caroms over so wide a spectrum in his Dior designs that it's still possible to be surprised.
           </p>
           <p>
            For the awards ceremony this evening, Ms. Cotillard, a nominee for "Two Days, One Night," selected a white Haute Couture gown, picking up on a minitrend of the evening: white dresses for black tie. It looked as good from the back, where it gathered with a black band, as it did from the front.
           </p>
           <p>
            <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/projects/awards-season/2014/red-carpet/marion-cotillard/">
             See more of her looks.
            </a>
           </p>
          </div>

          </h6>
          <h2 class="cp-celeb" itemprop="headline name">
           <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/rosamund-pike" itemprop="url">
            Rosamund Pike
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="cp-desc" itemprop="articleBody description text">
           <p>
            Does the carpet match the dress? For a few brave souls, yes. Ms. Pike, a nominee for "Gone Girl," chose lipstick-red Givenchy Haute Couture.
           </p>
           <p>
            It was a bold move, but Ms. Pike reaped the reward. Her strapless high-slit gown, if not one of the night's most exciting, was flattering and memorable. What's more, her red belt blended in and so didn't invite jabs from the online peanut gallery, as Nicole Kidman's did.
           </p>
           <p>
            <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/rosamund-pike">

         <div class="cp-text photo " id="cp-block-54ea6b3a61646d76db0a0000">
          <h6 class="cp-date">
           <a class="cp-date-a" datetime="2015-03-19T11:16:06+00:00" href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/felicity-jones">
            June 17, 2015
           </a>
          </h6>
          <h2 class="cp-celeb" itemprop="headline name">
           <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/felicity-jones" itemprop="url">
            Felicity Jones
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="cp-desc" itemprop="articleBody description text">
           <p>
            "Divisive" is the word for Ms. Jones's Alexander McQueen gown, which has fans and detractors in roughly equal measure. Or maybe "divided" is closer to the mark. The bodice of Ms. Jones's gown, detailed with what the brand called "3D flower embroidery," seemed high fashion; the sweeping skirt, bridal.
           </p>
           <p>
            Like it or hate it, you have to give her this much, at least: for a Best Actress nominee from a tear-jerker love story, it felt appropriately romantic.
           </p>
           <p>
            <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/felicity-jones">
             See more of her looks.
            </a>
           </p>
          </div>
          <ul class="cp-related">
          </ul>

          <h6 class="cp-date">
           <a class="cp-date-a" datetime="2015-03-19T11:16:06+00:00" href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/margot-robbie">
            June 17, 2015
           </a>
          </h6>
          <h2 class="cp-celeb" itemprop="headline name">
           <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/margot-robbie" itemprop="url">
            Margot Robbie
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="cp-desc" itemprop="articleBody description text">
           <p>
            Ms. Robbie, the breakout star of "The Wolf of Wall Street," soon to be beguiling Will Smith in "Focus," opening this week, went wily for the Academy Awards, in a plunging femme fatale look by Saint Laurent.
           </p>
           <p>
            Whopper necklaces have been one of the evening's minitrends  see also Scarlett Johansson, Cate Blanchett and Laura Dern  but Ms. Robbie's has provenance. It's a vintage Van Cleef &amp; Arpels, originally designed, she told the red-carpet fashion squad, for the Duchess of Windsor. "This necklace right here," she said, "is worth more than my life."
           </p>
          </div>
          <ul class="cp-related">
          </ul>
          <div aria-label="tools" class="tone-standard sharetools theme-classic sharetools-story-meta layout-horizontal" data-description="Ms. Robbie, the breakout star of &quot;The Wolf of Wall Street,&quot; soon to be beguiling Will Smith in &quot;Focus,&quot; opening this week, went wily for the Academy Awards, in a plunging femme fata..." data-media="http://i1.nyt.com/images/2015/02/22/fashion/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-4UVD/22-OSCARS-NOTEWORTHY-slide-4UVD-facebookJumbo.jpg" data-shares="facebook|,twitter|,pinterest|,show-all|more" data-slug="margot-robbie" data-title="Red Carpet Watch | Oscars 2015 | Margot Robbie | NYTimes.com" data-url="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/margot-robbie" role="group">

          <h6 class="cp-date">
           <a class="cp-date-a" datetime="2015-03-19T11:16:06+00:00" href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/patricia-arquette">
            June 17, 2015
           </a>
          </h6>
          <h2 class="cp-celeb" itemprop="headline name">
           <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/patricia-arquette" itemprop="url">
            Patricia Arquette
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="cp-desc" itemprop="articleBody description text">
           <p>
            Patricia Arquette, who won the Oscar for Best Supporting Actress, bypassed the usual red-carpet guessing game. She announced her intention to wear a gown by her friend, the designer Rosetta Getty, the Los Angeles-based designer, and, lo and behold, she did. "It was easy to design a dress for Patricia since we have been best friends for years," said Ms. Getty in a statement. "When we were young, we always dreamed about how she would be an actress and I would be a fashion designer." Dreams come true!
           </p>
           <p>

             See more of her looks
            </a>
           </p>

            </a>
            . It didn't take long to get its first red-carpet airing. Ms. Miller wore a navy guipure lace and floral macram from fall 2015. That's a big get for the house, and for Mr. Copping as the successor to the late Mr. de la Renta, who was beloved of starlets. Consider it a good sign for red carpets to come.

            </p>

         <div class="cp-text photo " id="cp-block-54ea5c3661646d6397020000">
          <h6 class="cp-date">
           <a class="cp-date-a" datetime="2015-03-19T11:16:06+00:00" href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/anna-kendrick">
            June 17, 2015
           </a>
          </h6>
          <h2 class="cp-celeb" itemprop="headline name">
           <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/projects/cp/red-carpet-watch/oscars-2015/anna-kendrick" itemprop="url">
            Anna Kendrick
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="cp-desc" itemprop="articleBody description text">
           <p>
            Ms. Kendrick, whether by accident or design, was one of the first A-listers to walk the carpet once the preshow cameras were rolling. It was a rare case of being fashionably early: Ms. Kendrick's coral silk georgette gown, a custom piece by the New York designer Thakoon Panichgul, dominated the early red-carpet conversation on Twitter. The commentariat was generally in favor of Ms. Kendrick's dress, though for my money, a little princessy, as Ms. Kendrick's recent choices for the big red-carpet moments generally are. (She was in a frothy Monique Lhuillier at the Golden Globes.) Maybe playing Cinderella in "Into the Woods" rubbed off?
           </p>
          </div>
          <ul class="cp-related">
          </ul>
          <div aria-label="tools" class="tone-standard sharetools theme-classic sharetools-story-meta layout-horizontal" data-description="Ms. Kendrick, whether by accident or design, was one of the first A-listers to walk the carpet once the preshow cameras were rolling.
